衣服	yīfu	A1	clothes; CL:件[jiàn],套[tào]

有	yǒu	A1	to have; there is; there are; to exist; to be
月	yuè	A1	moon; month; CL:個|个[gè],輪|轮[lún]
在	zài	A1	(located) at; (to be) in; to exist; in the middle of doing sth; (indicating an action in progress)
再见	zàijiàn	A1	goodbye; see you again later
怎么	zěnme	A1	how?; what?; why?
怎么样	zěnmeyàng	A1	how?; how about?; how was it?; how are things?
这	zhè	A1	this; these; (commonly pr. zhèi before a classifier, esp. in Beijing)
这儿	zhèr	A1	here

字	zì	A1	letter; symbol; character; word; CL:個|个[gè]; courtesy or style name traditionally given to males aged 2 in dynastic China
昨天	zuótiān	A1	yesterday
坐	zuò	A1	to sit; to take a seat; to take (a bus, airplane etc); to bear fruit; surname Zuo
做	zuò	A1	to do; to make; to produce; to write; to compose; to act as; to engage in; to hold (a party); to be; to become; to function (in some capacity); to serve as; to be used for; to form (a bond or relationship); to pretend; to feign; to act a part; to put on appearance
